ExpandQuantumRoot[\[CapitalGamma]_][SuperPlus[Subscript[X, \[CapitalGamma]_, 
       r_]]] /; MemberQ[SimpleRoots[\[CapitalGamma]], 
     PositiveRoots[\[CapitalGamma]][[r]]] := 
   SuperPlus[Subscript[X, Position[SimpleRoots[\[CapitalGamma]], 
       PositiveRoots[\[CapitalGamma]][[r]]][[1,1]]]]
 
ExpandQuantumRoot[\[CapitalGamma]_][SuperPlus[Subscript[X, \[CapitalGamma]_, 
      r_]]] := ExpandQuantumRoot[\[CapitalGamma]][
     SuperPlus[Subscript[X, \[CapitalGamma], r]]] = 
    With[{i = LongestWordDecomposition[\[CapitalGamma]]}, 
     DebugPrintHeld["Calculating ", ExpandQuantumRoot[\[CapitalGamma]][
        SuperPlus[Subscript[X, \[CapitalGamma], r]]]]; 
      BraidAction[\[CapitalGamma]][(Subscript[T, #1] & ) /@ Take[i, r - 1], 
       SuperPlus[Subscript[X, i[[r]]]]]]

       PositiveRoots[\[CapitalGamma]][[r]]][[1,1]]]]
